# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've successfully compiled a comprehensive analysis of the Firefox CSS layout engine reflow pipeline. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've identified and documented **45+ C++ source files** in mozilla-firefox/firefox that implement the three core components of the CSS layout engine reflow pipeline:

### **1. Frame Construction**
- **nsCSSFrameConstructor** - Creates frames from DOM nodes
- **nsFrameManager** - Manages the frame hierarchy

### **2. Block Layout Reflow**
- **nsBlockFrame** - Core block box reflow algorithm
- **BlockReflowState** - State tracking during block reflow
- **nsBlockReflowContext** - Helper for child block reflow
- **nsFloatManager** - Manages float positioning
- **nsLineLayout** - Inline line layout management
- **nsInlineFrame** - Inline frame reflow
- **nsLineBox** - Line box representation

### **3. Dirty Frame Invalidation**
- **RestyleManager** - Style change invalidation and frame dirtying
- **PresShell** - Top-level reflow coordinator with `FrameNeedsReflow()`
- **RetainedDisplayListBuilder** - Incremental display list invalidation tracking
- **nsFrameStateBits** - Frame dirty state bits management
- **nsAutoLayoutPhase** - Layout phase coordination

The complete answer with all files, symbols, call chains, and detailed narrative explanation has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json`.

components implemented across the layout/base, layout/generic, and layout/style directories:\\n\\n## 1. Frame Construction\\n\\nFrame construction is the initial process that creates the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in `nsCSSFrameConstructor` (layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h and .cpp), which extends `nsFrameManager` (layout/base/nsFrameManager.h and .cpp). This component converts styled DOM nodes into layout frames, handling anonymous frame generation for tables, flex containers, and other special layout modes.\\n\\n## 2. Block Layout Reflow\\n\\nThe block layout reflow implements the CSS Block Formatting Context (BFC) and handles the reflow of block-level frames. Key components include:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame** (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h and .cpp): Implements the core block box reflow algorithm that processes lines of inline content and handles floats, margins, padding, and borders.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState** (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h and .cpp): Maintains state information during block reflow, including margin collapsing calculations, float management, and line iteration.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext** (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h and .cpp): A helper class that computes reflow for child block frames within a parent block container.\\n\\n- **nsFloatManager** (layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h and .cpp): Manages float positioning and reserves space for floated elements within blocks.\\n\\nInline content reflow is handled by:\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout** (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h and .cpp): Manages the layout of inline content within lines.\\n- **nsInlineFrame** (layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h and .cpp): Handles reflow of inline and inline-block frames.\\n- **nsLineBox** (layout/generic/nsLineBox.h and .cpp): Represents a single line of inline content.\\n\\n## 3. Style changes trigger `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()`\\n2. `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()` applies style changes and marks frames dirty\\n3. `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` adds frames to the reflow queue\\n4. `PresShell::DoReflow()` calls frame `Reflow()` methods top-down\\n5. `nsBlockFrame::Reflow()` processes block layout with `BlockReflowState`\\n6. `nsInlineFrame::Reflow()` and `nsLineLayout` handle inline reflow\\n7. Float positioning is managed via `nsFloatManager`\\n8. `PresShell::DidReflow()` clears dirty bits after successful reflow\\n9. `RetainedDisplayListBuilder` tracks invalidation for the next paint cycle\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes `ReflowOutput` for reflow results, `nsPresContext` for presentation context state, and `nsLayoutUtils` utility functions for layout calculations.\"\n}\n",

components implemented across the layout/base, layout/generic, and layout/style directories:\\n\\n## 1. Frame Construction\\n\\nFrame construction is the initial process that creates the frame tree from the DOM tree. The primary implementation is in `nsCSSFrameConstructor` (layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.h and .cpp), which extends `nsFrameManager` (layout/base/nsFrameManager.h and .cpp). This component converts styled DOM nodes into layout frames, handling anonymous frame generation for tables, flex containers, and other special layout modes.\\n\\n## 2. Block Layout Reflow\\n\\nThe block layout reflow implements the CSS Block Formatting Context (BFC) and handles the reflow of block-level frames. Key components include:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame** (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.h and .cpp): Implements the core block box reflow algorithm that processes lines of inline content and handles floats, margins, padding, and borders.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState** (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.h and .cpp): Maintains state information during block reflow, including margin collapsing calculations, float management, and line iteration.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext** (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.h and .cpp): A helper class that computes reflow for child block frames within a parent block container.\\n\\n- **nsFloatManager** (layout/generic/nsFloatManager.h and .cpp): Manages float positioning and reserves space for floated elements within blocks.\\n\\nInline content reflow is handled by:\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout** (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.h and .cpp): Manages the layout of inline content within lines.\\n- **nsInlineFrame** (layout/generic/nsInlineFrame.h and .cpp): Handles reflow of inline and inline-block frames.\\n- **nsLineBox** (layout/generic/nsLineBox.h and .cpp): Represents a single line of inline content.\\n\\n## 3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism\\n\\nThe dirty frame invalidation system tracks which frames need reflow and ensures efficient incremental reflow:\\n\\n- **PresShell** (layout/base/PresShell.h and .cpp): The presentation shell is the top-level reflow coordinator that manages the reflow tree and calls `FrameNeedsReflow()` to schedule frames for reflow.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager** (layout/style/RestyleManager.h and .cpp): Manages style changes and invalidation, with `ProcessRestyledFrames()` handling the frame invalidation chain triggered by style updates.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput** (layout/generic/ReflowInput.h and .cpp): Encapsulates all input parameters needed for reflow, including available space, containing block size, and parent reflow state.\\n\\n- **RetainedDisplayListBuilder** (layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.h and .cpp): Tracks frame invalidation information for incremental display list construction.\\n\\n- **nsFrameStateBits** (layout/generic/nsFrameStateBits.h): Defines frame state bits including `NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY`, `NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN`, and `NS_BLOCK_LOOK_FOR_DIRTY_FRAMES` that mark frames needing reflow.\\n\\n- **nsAutoLayoutPhase** (layout/base/nsAutoLayoutPhase.h and .cpp): Manages layout phase tracking to prevent conflicting layout operations.\\n\\n## Reflow Data Flow\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline follows this sequence:\\n\\n1. Style changes trigger `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()`\\n2. `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames()` applies style changes and marks frames dirty\\n3. `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` adds frames to the reflow queue\\n4. `PresShell::DoReflow()` calls frame `Reflow()` methods top-down\\n5. `nsBlockFrame::Reflow()` processes block layout with `BlockReflowState`\\n6. `nsInlineFrame::Reflow()` and `nsLineLayout` handle inline reflow\\n7. Float positioning is managed via `nsFloatManager`\\n8. `PresShell::DidReflow()` clears dirty bits after successful reflow\\n9. `RetainedDisplayListBuilder` tracks invalidation for the next paint cycle\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes `ReflowOutput` for reflow results, `nsPresContext` for presentation context state, and `nsLayoutUtils` utility functions for layout calculations.\"\n}\n",
